<pr_description>
Streaming agents do not call the agent_end lifecycle hook
### Describe the bug

I need to collect usage information at the end of each of my agent runs. For non-streaming agents I can hook into the `agent_end` event and fetch the usage information from the run context. However for steaming agents, my handler is never called. 

### Debug information

- Agents SDK version: `v0.0.17`
- Runtime environment: `Node.js 20.19.3`

### Repro steps

```
const myAgent = new Agent({
    name: 'My Agent',
    instructions: 'Some instructions'
  });
const runner = new Runner();
const streamResult = await runner.run(myAgent, [], {
   context: {},
   stream: true
});
myAgent.on('agent_tool_start', () => {
  console.log('agent_tool_start called');  // This works!
);
myAgent.on('agent_tool_end', () => {
  console.log('agent_tool_end called');  // This function is never hit
);

```

### Expected behavior
I expect completed streaming agents to call the `agent_tool_end` handlers.



</pr_description>

    66	   * The model to use for the entire agent run. If set, will override the model set on every
    67	   * agent. The modelProvider passed in below must be able to resolve this model name.
    68	   */
    69	  model?: string | Model;
    70	
    71	  /**

    73	   */

    97	  outputGuardrails?: OutputGuardrail<AgentOutputType<unknown>>[];

   102	  tracingDisabled: boolean;

   105	   * Whether we include potentially sensitive data (for example: inputs/outputs of tool calls or

   108	   */

   134	type SharedRunOptions<TContext = undefined> = {
   135	  context?: TContext | RunContext<TContext>;
   136	  maxTurns?: number;

   141	export type StreamRunOptions<TContext = undefined> =
   142	  SharedRunOptions<TContext> & {
   143	    /**
   144	     * Whether to stream the run. If true, the run will emit events as the model responds.
   145	     */
   146	    stream: true;
   147	  };
   148

   150	  SharedRunOptions<TContext> & {
   151	    /**
   152	     * Whether to stream the run. If true, the run will emit events as the model responds.
   153	     */
   154	    stream?: false;
   155	  };
   156	
   157	export type IndividualRunOptions<TContext = undefined> =
   158	  | StreamRunOptions<TContext>
   159	  | NonStreamRunOptions<TContext>;
   160	
   161	/**
   162	 * @internal
   163	 */
   164	export function getTracing(
   165	  tracingDisabled: boolean,
   166	  traceIncludeSensitiveData: boolean,
   167	): ModelTracing {
   168	  if (tracingDisabled) {
   169	    return false;
   170	  }
   171	
   172	  if (traceIncludeSensitiveData) {
   173	    return true;
   174	  }
   175	
   176	  return 'enabled_without_data';
   177	}
   178	
   179	export function getTurnInput(
   180	  originalInput: string | AgentInputItem[],
   181	  generatedItems: RunItem[],
   182	): AgentInputItem[] {
   183	  const rawItems = generatedItems
   184	    .filter((item) => item.type !== 'tool_approval_item') // don't include approval items to avoid double function calls
   185	    .map((item) => item.rawItem);
   186	
   187	  if (typeof originalInput === 'string') {
   188	    originalInput = [{ type: 'message', role: 'user', content: originalInput }];
   189	  }
   190	
   191	  return [...originalInput, ...rawItems];
   192	}

   194	/**
   195	 * A Runner is responsible for running an agent workflow.
   196	 */
   197	export class Runner extends RunHooks<any, AgentOutputType<unknown>> {
   198	  public readonly config: RunConfig;
   199	  private readonly inputGuardrailDefs: InputGuardrailDefinition[];
   200	  private readonly outputGuardrailDefs: OutputGuardrailDefinition<
   201	    OutputGuardrailMetadata,

   203	  >[];

   208	      modelProvider: config.modelProvider ?? getDefaultModelProvider(),
   209	      model: config.model,
   210	      modelSettings: config.modelSettings,
   211	      handoffInputFilter: config.handoffInputFilter,
   212	      inputGuardrails: config.inputGuardrails,
   213	      outputGuardrails: config.outputGuardrails,
   214	      tracingDisabled: config.tracingDisabled ?? false,
   215	      traceIncludeSensitiveData: config.traceIncludeSensitiveData ?? true,
   216	      workflowName: config.workflowName ?? 'Agent workflow',
   217	      traceId: config.traceId,
   218	      groupId: config.groupId,
   219	      traceMetadata: config.traceMetadata,
   220	    };
   221	    this.inputGuardrailDefs = (config.inputGuardrails ?? []).map(
   222	      defineInputGuardrail,
   223	    );
   224	    this.outputGuardrailDefs = (config.outputGuardrails ?? []).map(
   225	      defineOutputGuardrail,
   226	    );
   227	  }
   228	
   229	  /**
   230	   * @internal
   231	   */
   232	  async #runIndividualNonStream<
   233	    TContext,
   234	    TAgent extends Agent<TContext, AgentOutputType>,
   235	    _THandoffs extends (Agent<any, any> | Handoff<any>)[] = any[],
   236	  >(
   237	    startingAgent: TAgent,
   238	    input: string | AgentInputItem[] | RunState<TContext, TAgent>,
   239	    options: NonStreamRunOptions<TContext>,
   240	  ): Promise<RunResult<TContext, TAgent>> {
   241	    return withNewSpanContext(async () => {
   242	      // if we have a saved state we use that one, otherwise we create a new one
   243	      const state =
   244	        input instanceof RunState
   245	          ? input
   246	          : new RunState(
   247	              options.context instanceof RunContext
   248	                ? options.context
   249	                : new RunContext(options.context),
   250	              input,
   251	              startingAgent,
   252	              options.maxTurns ?? DEFAULT_MAX_TURNS,
   253	            );
   254	
   255	      try {
   256	        while (true) {
   257	          const explictlyModelSet =
   258	            (state._currentAgent.model !== undefined &&
   259	              state._currentAgent.model !== '') ||
   260	            (this.config.model !== undefined && this.config.model !== '');
   261	          let model = selectModel(state._currentAgent.model, this.config.model);
   262	
   263	          if (typeof model === 'string') {
   264	            model = await this.config.modelProvider.getModel(model);
   265	          }
   266	
   267	          // if we don't have a current step, we treat this as a new run
   268	          state._currentStep = state._currentStep ?? {
   269	            type: 'next_step_run_again',
   270	          };
   271	
   272	          if (state._currentStep.type === 'next_step_interruption') {
   273	            logger.debug('Continuing from interruption');
   274	            if (!state._lastTurnResponse || !state._lastProcessedResponse) {
   275	              throw new UserError(
   276	                'No model response found in previous state',
   277	                state,
   278	              );
   279	            }
   280	
   281	            const turnResult =
   282	              await executeInterruptedToolsAndSideEffects<TContext>(
   283	                state._currentAgent,
   284	                state._originalInput,
   285	                state._generatedItems,
   286	                state._lastTurnResponse,
   287	                state._lastProcessedResponse as ProcessedResponse<unknown>,
   288	                this,
   289	                state,
   290	              );
   291	
   292	            state._toolUseTracker.addToolUse(
   293	              state._currentAgent,
   294	              state._lastProcessedResponse.toolsUsed,
   295	            );
   296	
   297	            state._originalInput = turnResult.originalInput;
   298	            state._generatedItems = turnResult.generatedItems;
   299	            state._currentStep = turnResult.nextStep;
   300	
   301	            if (turnResult.nextStep.type === 'next_step_interruption') {
   302	              // we are still in an interruption, so we need to avoid an infinite loop
   303	              return new RunResult<TContext, TAgent>(state);
   304	            }
   305	
   306	            continue;
   307	          }
   308	
   309	          if (state._currentStep.type === 'next_step_run_again') {
   310	            const handoffs: Handoff<any>[] = [];
   311	            if (state._currentAgent.handoffs) {
   312	              // While this array usually must not be undefined,
   313	              // we've added this check to prevent unexpected runtime errors like https://github.com/openai/openai-agents-js/issues/138
   314	              handoffs.push(...state._currentAgent.handoffs.map(getHandoff));
   315	            }
   316	
   317	            if (!state._currentAgentSpan) {
   318	              const handoffNames = handoffs.map((h) => h.agentName);
   319	              state._currentAgentSpan = createAgentSpan({
   320	                data: {
   321	                  name: state._currentAgent.name,
   322	                  handoffs: handoffNames,
   323	                  output_type: state._currentAgent.outputSchemaName,
   324	                },
   325	              });
   326	              state._currentAgentSpan.start();
   327	              setCurrentSpan(state._currentAgentSpan);
   328	            }
   329	
   330	            const tools = await state._currentAgent.getAllTools(state._context);
   331	            const serializedTools = tools.map((t) => serializeTool(t));
   332	            const serializedHandoffs = handoffs.map((h) => serializeHandoff(h));
   333	            if (state._currentAgentSpan) {
   334	              state._currentAgentSpan.spanData.tools = tools.map((t) => t.name);
   335	            }
   336	
   337	            state._currentTurn++;
   338	
   339	            if (state._currentTurn > state._maxTurns) {
   340	              state._currentAgentSpan?.setError({
   341	                message: 'Max turns exceeded',
   342	                data: { max_turns: state._maxTurns },
   343	              });
   344	
   345	              throw new MaxTurnsExceededError(
   346	                `Max turns (${state._maxTurns}) exceeded`,
   347	                state,
   348	              );
   349	            }
   350	
   351	            logger.debug(
   352	              `Running agent ${state._currentAgent.name} (turn ${state._currentTurn})`,
   353	            );
   354	
   355	            if (state._currentTurn === 1) {
   356	              await this.#runInputGuardrails(state);
   357	            }
   358	
   359	            const turnInput = getTurnInput(
   360	              state._originalInput,
   361	              state._generatedItems,
   362	            );
   363	
   364	            if (state._noActiveAgentRun) {
   365	              state._currentAgent.emit(
   366	                'agent_start',
   367	                state._context,
   368	                state._currentAgent,
   369	              );
   370	              this.emit('agent_start', state._context, state._currentAgent);
   371	            }
   372	
   373	            let modelSettings = {
   374	              ...this.config.modelSettings,
   375	              ...state._currentAgent.modelSettings,
   376	            };
   377	            const agentModelSettings = state._currentAgent.modelSettings;
   378	            modelSettings = adjustModelSettingsForNonGPT5RunnerModel(
   379	              explictlyModelSet,
   380	              agentModelSettings,
   381	              model,
   382	              modelSettings,
   383	            );
   384	            modelSettings = maybeResetToolChoice(
   385	              state._currentAgent,
   386	              state._toolUseTracker,
   387	              modelSettings,
   388	            );
   389	            state._lastTurnResponse = await model.getResponse({
   390	              systemInstructions: await state._currentAgent.getSystemPrompt(
   391	                state._context,
   392	              ),
   393	              prompt: await state._currentAgent.getPrompt(state._context),
   394	              input: turnInput,
   395	              previousResponseId: options.previousResponseId,
   396	              modelSettings,
   397	              tools: serializedTools,
   398	              outputType: convertAgentOutputTypeToSerializable(
   399	                state._currentAgent.outputType,
   400	              ),
   401	              handoffs: serializedHandoffs,
   402	              tracing: getTracing(
   403	                this.config.tracingDisabled,
   404	                this.config.traceIncludeSensitiveData,
   405	              ),
   406	              signal: options.signal,
   407	            });
   408	            state._modelResponses.push(state._lastTurnResponse);
   409	            state._context.usage.add(state._lastTurnResponse.usage);
   410	            state._noActiveAgentRun = false;
   411	
   412	            const processedResponse = processModelResponse(
   413	              state._lastTurnResponse,
   414	              state._currentAgent,
   415	              tools,
   416	              handoffs,
   417	            );
   418	
   419	            state._lastProcessedResponse = processedResponse;
   420	            const turnResult = await executeToolsAndSideEffects<TContext>(
   421	              state._currentAgent,
   422	              state._originalInput,
   423	              state._generatedItems,
   424	              state._lastTurnResponse,
   425	              state._lastProcessedResponse,
   426	              this,
   427	              state,
   428	            );
   429	
   430	            state._toolUseTracker.addToolUse(
   431	              state._currentAgent,
   432	              state._lastProcessedResponse.toolsUsed,
   433	            );
   434	
   435	            state._originalInput = turnResult.originalInput;
   436	            state._generatedItems = turnResult.generatedItems;
   437	            state._currentStep = turnResult.nextStep;
   438	          }
   439	
   440	          if (
   441	            state._currentStep &&
   442	            state._currentStep.type === 'next_step_final_output'
   443	          ) {
   444	            await this.#runOutputGuardrails(state, state._currentStep.output);
   445	            this.emit(
   446	              'agent_end',
   447	              state._context,
   448	              state._currentAgent,
   449	              state._currentStep.output,
   450	            );
   451	            state._currentAgent.emit(
   452	              'agent_end',
   453	              state._context,
   454	              state._currentStep.output,
   455	            );
   456	            return new RunResult<TContext, TAgent>(state);
   457	          } else if (
   458	            state._currentStep &&
   459	            state._currentStep.type === 'next_step_handoff'
   460	          ) {
   461	            state._currentAgent = state._currentStep.newAgent as TAgent;
   462	            if (state._currentAgentSpan) {
   463	              state._currentAgentSpan.end();
   464	              resetCurrentSpan();
   465	              state._currentAgentSpan = undefined;
   466	            }
   467	            state._noActiveAgentRun = true;
   468	
   469	            // we've processed the handoff, so we need to run the loop again
   470	            state._currentStep = { type: 'next_step_run_again' };
   471	          } else if (
   472	            state._currentStep &&
   473	            state._currentStep.type === 'next_step_interruption'
   474	          ) {

    72	/**
    73	 * @internal
    74	 */
    75	export function processModelResponse<TContext>(
    76	  modelResponse: ModelResponse,
    77	  agent: Agent<any, any>,
    78	  tools: Tool<TContext>[],
    79	  handoffs: Handoff[],
    80	): ProcessedResponse<TContext> {
    81	  const items: RunItem[] = [];
    82	  const runHandoffs: ToolRunHandoff[] = [];
    83	  const runFunctions: ToolRunFunction<TContext>[] = [];
    84	  const runComputerActions: ToolRunComputer[] = [];
    85	  const runMCPApprovalRequests: ToolRunMCPApprovalRequest[] = [];
    86	  const toolsUsed: string[] = [];
    87	  const handoffMap = new Map(handoffs.map((h) => [h.toolName, h]));
    88	  const functionMap = new Map(
    89	    tools.filter((t) => t.type === 'function').map((t) => [t.name, t]),
    90	  );
    91	  const computerTool = tools.find((t) => t.type === 'computer');
    92	  const mcpToolMap = new Map(
    93	    tools
    94	      .filter((t) => t.type === 'hosted_tool' && t.providerData?.type === 'mcp')
    95	      .map((t) => t as HostedMCPTool)
    96	      .map((t) => [t.providerData.server_label, t]),
    97	  );
    98	
    99	  for (const output of modelResponse.output) {
   100	    if (output.type === 'message') {
   101	      if (output.role === 'assistant') {
   102	        items.push(new RunMessageOutputItem(output, agent));
   103	      }
   104	    } else if (output.type === 'hosted_tool_call') {
   105	      items.push(new RunToolCallItem(output, agent));

   108	
   109	      if (
   110	        output.providerData?.type === 'mcp_approval_request' ||
   111	        output.name === 'mcp_approval_request'
   112	      ) {
   113	        // Hosted remote MCP server's approval process
   114	        const providerData =
   115	          output.providerData as ProviderData.HostedMCPApprovalRequest;
   116	
   117	        const mcpServerLabel = providerData.server_label;
   118	        const mcpServerTool = mcpToolMap.get(mcpServerLabel);
   119	        if (typeof mcpServerTool === 'undefined') {
   120	          const message = `MCP server (${mcpServerLabel}) not found in Agent (${agent.name})`;
   121	          addErrorToCurrentSpan({
   122	            message,
   123	            data: { mcp_server_label: mcpServerLabel },
   124	          });
   125	          throw new ModelBehaviorError(message);
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        // Do this approval later:
   129	        // We support both onApproval callback (like the Python SDK does) and HITL patterns.
   130	        const approvalItem = new RunToolApprovalItem(
   131	          {
   132	            type: 'hosted_tool_call',
   133	            // We must use this name to align with the name sent from the servers
   134	            name: providerData.name,
   135	            id: providerData.id,
   136	            status: 'in_progress',
   137	            providerData,
   138	          },
   139	          agent,
   140	        );
   141	        runMCPApprovalRequests.push({
   142	          requestItem: approvalItem,
   143	          mcpTool: mcpServerTool,
   144	        });
   145	        if (!mcpServerTool.providerData.on_approval) {
   146	          // When onApproval function exists, it confirms the approval right after this.
   147	          // Thus, this approval item must be appended only for the next turn interruption patterns.
   148	          items.push(approvalItem);
   149	        }
   150	      }
   151	    } else if (output.type === 'reasoning') {
   152	      items.push(new RunReasoningItem(output, agent));
   153	    } else if (output.type === 'computer_call') {
   154	      items.push(new RunToolCallItem(output, agent));
   155	      toolsUsed.push('computer_use');
   156	      if (!computerTool) {
   157	        addErrorToCurrentSpan({
   158	          message: 'Model produced computer action without a computer tool.',
   159	          data: {
   160	            agent_name: agent.name,
   161	          },
   162	        });
   163	        throw new ModelBehaviorError(
   164	          'Model produced computer action without a computer tool.',
   165	        );
   166	      }
   167	      runComputerActions.push({
   168	        toolCall: output,
   169	        computer: computerTool,
   170	      });
   171	    }
   172	
   173	    if (output.type !== 'function_call') {
   174	      continue;
   175	    }
   176	
   177	    toolsUsed.push(output.name);
   178	
   179	    const handoff = handoffMap.get(output.name);
   180	    if (handoff) {
   181	      items.push(new RunHandoffCallItem(output, agent));
   182	      runHandoffs.push({
   183	        toolCall: output,
   184	        handoff: handoff,
   185	      });
   186	    } else {
   187	      const functionTool = functionMap.get(output.name);
   188	      if (!functionTool) {
   189	        addErrorToCurrentSpan({
   190	          message: `Tool ${output.name} not found in agent ${agent.name}.`,
   191	          data: {
   192	            tool_name: output.name,
   193	            agent_name: agent.name,
   194	          },
   195	        });
   196	
   197	        throw new ModelBehaviorError(
   198	          `Tool ${output.name} not found in agent ${agent.name}.`,
   199	        );
   200	      }
   201	      items.push(new RunToolCallItem(output, agent));
   202	      runFunctions.push({
   203	        toolCall: output,
   204	        tool: functionTool,
   205	      });
   206	    }
   207	  }
   208	
   209	  return {
   210	    newItems: items,
   211	    handoffs: runHandoffs,
   212	    functions: runFunctions,
   213	    computerActions: runComputerActions,
   214	    mcpApprovalRequests: runMCPApprovalRequests,
   215	    toolsUsed: toolsUsed,
   216	    hasToolsOrApprovalsToRun(): boolean {
   217	      return (
   218	        runHandoffs.length > 0 ||
   219	        runFunctions.length > 0 ||
   220	        runMCPApprovalRequests.length > 0 ||
   221	        runComputerActions.length > 0
   222	      );
   223	    },
   224	  };
   225	}
   226	
   227	export const nextStepSchema = z.discriminatedUnion('type', [
   228	  z.object({
   229	    type: z.literal('next_step_handoff'),
   230	    newAgent: z.any(),
   231	  }),
   232	  z.object({
   233	    type: z.literal('next_step_final_output'),
   234	    output: z.string(),
   235	  }),
   236	  z.object({
   237	    type: z.literal('next_step_run_again'),
   238	  }),
   239	  z.object({
   240	    type: z.literal('next_step_interruption'),
   241	    data: z.record(z.string(), z.any()),
   242	  }),
   243	]);
   244	
   245	export type NextStep = z.infer<typeof nextStepSchema>;
   246	
   247	class SingleStepResult {
   248	  constructor(
   249	    /**
   250	     * The input items i.e. the items before run() was called. May be muted by handoff input filters
   251	     */
   252	    public originalInput: string | AgentInputItem[],
   253	    /**
   254	     * The model response for the current step
   255	     */
   256	    public modelResponse: ModelResponse,
   257	    /**
   258	     * The items before the current step was executed
   259	     */
   260	    public preStepItems: RunItem[],
   261	    /**
   262	     * The items after the current step was executed
   263	     */
   264	    public newStepItems: RunItem[],
   265	    /**
   266	     * The next step to execute
   267	     */
   268	    public nextStep: NextStep,
   269	  ) {}
   270	
   271	  /**
   272	   * The items generated during the agent run (i.e. everything generated after originalInput)
   273	   */
   274	  get generatedItems(): RunItem[] {
   275	    return this.preStepItems.concat(this.newStepItems);
   276	  }
   277	}
   278	
   279	/**
   280	 * @internal
   281	 */
   282	export function maybeResetToolChoice(
   283	  agent: Agent<any, any>,
   284	  toolUseTracker: AgentToolUseTracker,
   285	  modelSettings: ModelSettings,
   286	) {
   287	  if (agent.resetToolChoice && toolUseTracker.hasUsedTools(agent)) {
   288	    return { ...modelSettings, toolChoice: undefined };
   289	  }
   290	  return modelSettings;
   291	}
   292	
   293	/**
   294	 * @internal
   295	 */
   296	export async function executeInterruptedToolsAndSideEffects<TContext>(
   297	  agent: Agent<TContext, any>,
   298	  originalInput: string | AgentInputItem[],
   299	  originalPreStepItems: RunItem[],
   300	  newResponse: ModelResponse,
   301	  processedResponse: ProcessedResponse,
   302	  runner: Runner,
   303	  state: RunState<TContext, Agent<TContext, any>>,
   304	): Promise<SingleStepResult> {
   305	  // call_ids for function tools
   306	  const functionCallIds = originalPreStepItems
   307	    .filter(
   308	      (item) =>
   309	        item instanceof RunToolApprovalItem &&
   310	        'callId' in item.rawItem &&
   311	        item.rawItem.type === 'function_call',
   312	    )
   313	    .map((item) => (item.rawItem as protocol.FunctionCallItem).callId);
   314	  // Run function tools that require approval after they get their approval results
   315	  const functionToolRuns = processedResponse.functions.filter((run) => {
   316	    return functionCallIds.includes(run.toolCall.callId);
   317	  });
   318	
   319	  const functionResults = await executeFunctionToolCalls(
   320	    agent,
   321	    functionToolRuns,
   322	    runner,
   323	    state,
   324	  );
   325	
   326	  // Create the initial set of the output items
   327	  const newItems: RunItem[] = functionResults.map((r) => r.runItem);
   328	
   329	  // Run MCP tools that require approval after they get their approval results
   330	  const mcpApprovalRuns = processedResponse.mcpApprovalRequests.filter(
   331	    (run) => {
   332	      return (
   333	        run.requestItem.type === 'tool_approval_item' &&
   334	        run.requestItem.rawItem.type === 'hosted_tool_call' &&
   335	        run.requestItem.rawItem.providerData?.type === 'mcp_approval_request'
   336	      );
   337	    },
   338	  );
   339	  for (const run of mcpApprovalRuns) {
   340	    // the approval_request_id "mcpr_123..."
   341	    const approvalRequestId = run.requestItem.rawItem.id!;
   342	    const approved = state._context.isToolApproved({
   343	      // Since this item name must be the same with the one sent from Responses API server
   344	      toolName: run.requestItem.rawItem.name,
   345	      callId: approvalRequestId,
   346	    });
   347	    if (typeof approved !== 'undefined') {
   348	      const providerData: ProviderData.HostedMCPApprovalResponse = {
   349	        approve: approved,
   350	        approval_request_id: approvalRequestId,
   351	        reason: undefined,
   352	      };
   353	      // Tell Responses API server the approval result in the next turn
   354	      newItems.push(
   355	        new RunToolCallItem(
   356	          {
   357	            type: 'hosted_tool_call',
   358	            name: 'mcp_approval_response',
   359	            providerData,
   360	          },
   361	          agent as Agent<unknown, 'text'>,
   362	        ),
   363	      );
   364	    }
   365	  }
   366	
   367	  const checkToolOutput = await checkForFinalOutputFromTools(
   368	    agent,
   369	    functionResults,
   370	    state,
   371	  );
   372	
   373	  // Exclude the tool approval items, which should not be sent to Responses API,
   374	  // from the SingleStepResult's preStepItems
   375	  const preStepItems = originalPreStepItems.filter((item) => {
   376	    return !(item instanceof RunToolApprovalItem);
   377	  });
   378	
   379	  if (checkToolOutput.isFinalOutput) {
   380	    runner.emit(
   381	      'agent_end',
   382	      state._context,
   383	      agent,
   384	      checkToolOutput.finalOutput,
   385	    );
   386	    agent.emit('agent_end', state._context, checkToolOutput.finalOutput);
   387	
   388	    return new SingleStepResult(
   389	      originalInput,
   390	      newResponse,
   391	      preStepItems,
   392	      newItems,
   393	      {
   394	        type: 'next_step_final_output',
   395	        output: checkToolOutput.finalOutput,
   396	      },
   397	    );
   398	  } else if (checkToolOutput.isInterrupted) {
   399	    return new SingleStepResult(
   400	      originalInput,
   401	      newResponse,
   402	      preStepItems,
   403	      newItems,
   404	      {
   405	        type: 'next_step_interruption',
   406	        data: {
   407	          interruptions: checkToolOutput.interruptions,
   408	        },
   409	      },
   410	    );
   411	  }
   412	
   413	  // we only ran new tools and side effects. We need to run the rest of the agent
   414	  return new SingleStepResult(
   415	    originalInput,
   416	    newResponse,
   417	    preStepItems,
   418	    newItems,
   419	    { type: 'next_step_run_again' },
   420	  );
   421	}
   422	
   423	/**
   424	 * @internal
   425	 */
   426	export async function executeToolsAndSideEffects<TContext>(
   427	  agent: Agent<TContext, any>,
   428	  originalInput: string | AgentInputItem[],
   429	  originalPreStepItems: RunItem[],
   430	  newResponse: ModelResponse,
   431	  processedResponse: ProcessedResponse<TContext>,
   432	  runner: Runner,
   433	  state: RunState<TContext, Agent<TContext, any>>,
   434	): Promise<SingleStepResult> {
   435	  const preStepItems = originalPreStepItems;
   436	  let newItems = processedResponse.newItems;
   437	
   438	  const [functionResults, computerResults] = await Promise.all([
   439	    executeFunctionToolCalls(
   440	      agent,
   441	      processedResponse.functions as ToolRunFunction<unknown>[],
   442	      runner,
   443	      state,
   444	    ),
   445	    executeComputerActions(
   446	      agent,
   447	      processedResponse.computerActions,
   448	      runner,
   449	      state._context,
   450	    ),
   451	  ]);
   452	
   453	  newItems = newItems.concat(functionResults.map((r) => r.runItem));
   454	  newItems = newItems.concat(computerResults);
   455	
   456	  // run hosted MCP approval requests
   457	  if (processedResponse.mcpApprovalRequests.length > 0) {
   458	    for (const approvalRequest of processedResponse.mcpApprovalRequests) {
   459	      const toolData = approvalRequest.mcpTool
   460	        .providerData as ProviderData.HostedMCPTool<TContext>;
   461	      const requestData = approvalRequest.requestItem.rawItem
   462	        .providerData as ProviderData.HostedMCPApprovalRequest;
   463	      if (toolData.on_approval) {
   464	        // synchronously handle the approval process here
   465	        const approvalResult = await toolData.on_approval(
   466	          state._context,
   467	          approvalRequest.requestItem,
   468	        );
   469	        const approvalResponseData: ProviderData.HostedMCPApprovalResponse = {
   470	          approve: approvalResult.approve,
   471	          approval_request_id: requestData.id,
   472	          reason: approvalResult.reason,
   473	        };
   474	        newItems.push(
   475	          new RunToolCallItem(
   476	            {
   477	              type: 'hosted_tool_call',
   478	              name: 'mcp_approval_response',
   479	              providerData: approvalResponseData,
   480	            },
   481	            agent as Agent<unknown, 'text'>,
   482	          ),
   483	        );
   484	      } else {
   485	        // receive a user's approval on the next turn
   486	        newItems.push(approvalRequest.requestItem);
   487	        const approvalItem = {
   488	          type: 'hosted_mcp_tool_approval' as const,
   489	          tool: approvalRequest.mcpTool,
   490	          runItem: new RunToolApprovalItem(
   491	            {
   492	              type: 'hosted_tool_call',
   493	              name: requestData.name,
   494	              id: requestData.id,
   495	              arguments: requestData.arguments,
   496	              status: 'in_progress',
   497	              providerData: requestData,
   498	            },
   499	            agent,
   500	          ),
   501	        };
   502	        functionResults.push(approvalItem);
   503	        // newItems.push(approvalItem.runItem);
   504	      }
   505	    }
   506	  }
   507	
   508	  // process handoffs
   509	  if (processedResponse.handoffs.length > 0) {
   510	    return await executeHandoffCalls(
   511	      agent,
   512	      originalInput,
   513	      preStepItems,
   514	      newItems,
   515	      newResponse,
   516	      processedResponse.handoffs,
   517	      runner,
   518	      state._context,
   519	    );
   520	  }
   521	
   522	  const checkToolOutput = await checkForFinalOutputFromTools(
   523	    agent,
   524	    functionResults,
   525	    state,
   526	  );
   527	
   528	  if (checkToolOutput.isFinalOutput) {
   529	    runner.emit(
   530	      'agent_end',
   531	      state._context,
   532	      agent,
   533	      checkToolOutput.finalOutput,
   534	    );
   535	 <response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

    11	
    12	export abstract class EventEmitterDelegate<
    13	  EventTypes extends EventEmitterEvents = Record<string, any[]>,
    14	> implements EventEmitter<EventTypes>
    15	{
    16	  protected abstract eventEmitter: EventEmitter<EventTypes>;
    17	
    18	  on<K extends keyof EventTypes>(
    19	    type: K,
    20	    listener: (...args: EventTypes[K]) => void,
    21	  ): EventEmitter<EventTypes> {
    22	    this.eventEmitter.on(type, listener);
    23	    return this.eventEmitter;
    24	  }
    25	  off<K extends keyof EventTypes>(
    26	    type: K,
    27	    listener: (...args: EventTypes[K]) => void,
    28	  ): EventEmitter<EventTypes> {
    29	    this.eventEmitter.off(type, listener);
    30	    return this.eventEmitter;
    31	  }
    32	  emit<K extends keyof EventTypes>(type: K, ...args: EventTypes[K]): boolean {
    33	    return this.eventEmitter.emit(type, ...args);
    34	  }
    35	  once<K extends keyof EventTypes>(
    36	    type: K,
    37	    listener: (...args: EventTypes[K]) => void,
    38	  ): EventEmitter<EventTypes> {
    39	    this.eventEmitter.once(type, listener);
    40	    return this.eventEmitter;
    41	  }
    42	}

class MockModel extends Model {

    super('"'"'mock-model'"'"');
  }
  async getResponse(): Promise<ModelResponse> {
    return {
      output: [{ type: '"'"'message'"'"', role: '"'"'assistant'"'"', content: '"'"'Hello'"'"' }],
      usage: { promptTokens: 0, completionTokens: 0, totalTokens: 0 },
    };

        type: '"'"'response_done'"'"',

            id: '"'"'resp-1'"'"',

        }
    } as any;
  }

async function repro() {
  const myAgent = new Agent({
    name: '"'"'My Agent'"'"',
    instructions: '"'"'Some instructions'"'"',
    model: new MockModel(),
  });
  const runner = new Runner();
  
  let agentEndCalled = false;
  myAgent.on('"'"'agent_end'"'"', (context, output) => {
    console.log('"'"'agent_end called'"'"');
    agentEndCalled = true;
  });

  console.log('"'"'Running non-streaming agent...'"'"');
  await runner.run(myAgent, '"'"'hi'"'"', { stream: false });
  console.log('"'"'Non-streaming agent_end called:'"'"', agentEndCalled);

  agentEndCalled = false;
  console.log('"'"'\nRunning streaming agent...'"'"');
  const streamResult = await runner.run(myAgent, '"'"'hi'"'"', {
    stream: true
  });
  
  for await (const event of streamResult) {
    // consume stream
  }
  console.log('"'"'Streaming agent_end called:'"'"', agentEndCalled);
}

repro().catch(console.error);

import { Usage } from './usage';
import { StreamEvent } from './types/protocol';
import { HostedTool, ComputerTool, FunctionTool } from './tool';
import { Handoff } from './handoff';
import {
  AgentInputItem,
  AgentOutputItem,
  JsonSchemaDefinition,
  TextOutput,
  InputText,
  InputImage,
  InputFile,
} from './types';

export type ModelSettingsToolChoice =
  | 'auto'
  | 'required'
  | 'none'
  | (string & {});

/**
 * Settings to use when calling an LLM.
 *
 * This class holds optional model configuration parameters (e.g. temperature,
 * topP, penalties, truncation, etc.).
 *
 * Not all models/providers support all of these parameters, so please check the API documentation
 * for the specific model and provider you are using.
 */
export type ModelSettings = {
  /**
   * The temperature to use when calling the model.
   */
  temperature?: number;

  /**
   * The topP to use when calling the model.
   */
  topP?: number;

  /**
   * The frequency penalty to use when calling the model.
   */
  frequencyPenalty?: number;

  /**
   * The presence penalty to use when calling the model.
   */
  presencePenalty?: number;

  /**
   * The tool choice to use when calling the model.
   */
  toolChoice?: ModelSettingsToolChoice;

  /**
   * Whether to use parallel tool calls when calling the model.
   * Defaults to false if not provided.
   */
  parallelToolCalls?: boolean;

  /**
   * The truncation strategy to use when calling the model.
   */
  truncation?: 'auto' | 'disabled';

  /**
   * The maximum number of output tokens to generate.
   */
  maxTokens?: number;

  /**
   * Whether to store the generated model response for later retrieval.
   * Defaults to true if not provided.
   */
  store?: boolean;

  /**
   * Additional provider specific settings to be passed directly to the model
   * request.
   */
  providerData?: Record<string, any>;
};

export type ModelTracing = boolean | 'enabled_without_data';

export type SerializedFunctionTool = {
  /**
   * The type of the tool.
   */
  type: FunctionTool['type'];

  /**
   * The name of the tool.
   */
  name: FunctionTool['name'];

  /**
   * The description of the tool that helps the model to understand when to use the tool
   */
  description: FunctionTool['description'];

  /**
   * A JSON schema describing the parameters of the tool.
   */
  parameters: FunctionTool['parameters'];

  /**
   * Whether the tool is strict. If true, the model must try to strictly follow the schema
   * (might result in slower response times).
   */
  strict: FunctionTool['strict'];
};

export type SerializedComputerTool = {
  type: ComputerTool['type'];
  name: ComputerTool['name'];
  environment: ComputerTool['computer']['environment'];
  dimensions: ComputerTool['computer']['dimensions'];
};

export type SerializedHostedTool = {
  type: HostedTool['type'];
  name: HostedTool['name'];
  providerData?: HostedTool['providerData'];
};

export type SerializedTool =
  | SerializedFunctionTool
  | SerializedComputerTool
  | SerializedHostedTool;

export type SerializedHandoff = {
  /**
   * The name of the tool that represents the handoff.
   */
  toolName: Handoff['toolName'];

  /**
   * The tool description for the handoff
   */
  toolDescription: Handoff['toolDescription'];

  /**
   * The JSON schema for the handoff input. Can be empty if the handoff does not take an input
   */
  inputJsonSchema: Handoff['inputJsonSchema'];

  /**
   * Whether the input JSON schema is in strict mode. We strongly recommend setting this to true,
   * as it increases the likelihood of correct JSON input.
   */
  strictJsonSchema: Handoff['strictJsonSchema'];
};

/**
 * The output type passed to the model. Has any Zod types serialized to JSON Schema
 */
export type SerializedOutputType = JsonSchemaDefinition | TextOutput;

/**
 * A request to a large language model.
 */
export type ModelRequest = {
  /**
   * The system instructions to use for the model.
   */
  systemInstructions?: string;

  /**
   * The input to the model.
   */
  input: string | AgentInputItem[];

  /**
   * The ID of the previous response to use for the model.
   */
  previousResponseId?: string;

  /**
   * The model settings to use for the model.
   */
  modelSettings: ModelSettings;

  /**
   * The tools to use for the model.
   */
  tools: SerializedTool[];

  /**
   * The type of the output to use for the model.
   */
  outputType: SerializedOutputType;

  /**
   * The handoffs to use for the model.
   */
  handoffs: SerializedHandoff[];

  /**
   * Whether to enable tracing for the model.
   */
  tracing: ModelTracing;

  /**
   * An optional signal to abort the model request.
   */
  signal?: AbortSignal;

  /**
   * The prompt template to use for the model, if any.
   */
  prompt?: Prompt;
};

export type ModelResponse = {
  /**
   * The usage information for response.
   */
  usage: Usage;

  /**
   * A list of outputs (messages, tool calls, etc.) generated by the model.
   */
  output: AgentOutputItem[];

  /**
   * An ID for the response which can be used to refer to the response in subsequent calls to the
   * model. Not supported by all model providers.
   */
  responseId?: string;

  /**
   * Raw response data from the underlying model provider.
   */
  providerData?: Record<string, any>;
};

/**
 * The base interface for calling an LLM.
 */
export interface Model {
  /**
   * Get a response from the model.
   *
   * @param request - The request to get a response for.
   */
  getResponse(request: ModelRequest): Promise<ModelResponse>;

  /**
   * Get a streamed response from the model.
   *
   */
  getStreamedResponse(request: ModelRequest): AsyncIterable<StreamEvent>;
}

/**
 * The base interface for a model provider.
 *
 * The model provider is responsible for looking up `Model` instances by name.
 */
export interface ModelProvider {
  /**
   * Get a model by name
   *
   * @param modelName - The name of the model to get.
   */
  getModel(modelName?: string): Promise<Model> | Model;
}

/**
 * Reference to a prompt template and its variables.
 */
export type Prompt = {
  /**
   * The unique identifier of the prompt template to use.
   */
  promptId: string;
  /**
   * Optional version of the prompt template.
   */
  version?: string;
  /**
   * Optional variables to substitute into the prompt template.
   * Can be a string, or an object with string keys and values that are string,
   * InputText, InputImage, or InputFile.
   */
  variables?: {
    [key: string]: string | InputText | InputImage | InputFile;
  };
};

   221	   *   and gets to respond.
   222	   * - stop_on_first_tool: The output of the first tool call is used as the final output. This means
   223	   *   that the LLM does not process the result of the tool call.
   224	   * - A list of tool names: The agent will stop running if any of the tools in the list are called.
   225	   *   The final output will be the output of the first matching tool call. The LLM does not process
   226	   *   the result of the tool call.
   227	   * - A function: if you pass a function, it will be called with the run context and the list of
   228	   *   tool results. It must return a `ToolsToFinalOutputResult`, which determines whether the tool
   229	   *   call resulted in a final output.
   230	   *
   231	   * NOTE: This configuration is specific to `FunctionTools`. Hosted tools, such as file search, web
   232	   * search, etc. are always processed by the LLM
   233	   */
   234	  toolUseBehavior: ToolUseBehavior;
   235	
   236	  /**
   237	   * Whether to reset the tool choice to the default value after a tool has been called. Defaults
   238	   * to `true`. This ensures that the agent doesn't enter an infinite loop of tool usage.
   239	   */
   240	  resetToolChoice: boolean;
   241	}
   242	
   243	export type AgentOptions<
   244	  TContext = UnknownContext,
   245	  TOutput extends AgentOutputType = TextOutput,
   246	> = Expand<
   247	  Pick<AgentConfiguration<TContext, TOutput>, 'name'> &
   248	    Partial<AgentConfiguration<TContext, TOutput>>
   249	>;
   250	
   251	/**
   252	 * An agent is an AI model configured with instructions, tools, guardrails, handoffs and more.
   253	 *
   254	 * We strongly recommend passing `instructions`, which is the "system prompt" for the agent. In
   255	 * addition, you can pass `handoffDescription`, which is a human-readable description of the
   256	 * agent, used when the agent is used inside tools/handoffs.
   257	 *
   258	 * Agents are generic on the context type. The context is a (mutable) object you create. It is
   259	 * passed to tool functions, handoffs, guardrails, etc.
   260	 */
   261	// --- Type utilities for inferring output type from handoffs ---
   262	type ExtractAgentOutput<T> = T extends Agent<any, infer O> ? O : never;
   263	type ExtractHandoffOutput<T> = T extends Handoff<any, infer O> ? O : never;
   264	export type HandoffsOutputUnion<
   265	  Handoffs extends readonly (Agent<any, any> | Handoff<any, any>)[],
   266	> =
   267	  | ExtractAgentOutput<Handoffs[number]>
   268	  | ExtractHandoffOutput<Handoffs[number]>;
   269	
   270	/**
   271	 * Helper type for config with handoffs
   272	 *
   273	 * @template TOutput The type of the output object.
   274	 * @template Handoffs The type of the handoffs.
   275	 */
   276	export type AgentConfigWithHandoffs<
   277	  TOutput extends AgentOutputType,
   278	  Handoffs extends readonly (Agent<any, any> | Handoff<any, any>)[],
   279	> = { name: string; handoffs?: Handoffs; outputType?: TOutput } & Partial<
   280	  Omit<
   281	    AgentConfiguration<UnknownContext, TOutput | HandoffsOutputUnion<Handoffs>>,
   282	    'name' | 'handoffs' | 'outputType'
   283	  >
   284	>;
   285	
   286	/**
   287	 * The class representing an AI agent configured with instructions, tools, guardrails, handoffs and more.
   288	 *
   289	 * We strongly recommend passing `instructions`, which is the "system prompt" for the agent. In
   290	 * addition, you can pass `handoffDescription`, which is a human-readable description of the
   291	 * agent, used when the agent is used inside tools/handoffs.
   292	 *
   293	 * Agents are generic on the context type. The context is a (mutable) object you create. It is
   294	 * passed to tool functions, handoffs, guardrails, etc.
   295	 */
   296	export class Agent<
   297	    TContext = UnknownContext,
   298	    TOutput extends AgentOutputType = TextOutput,
   299	  >
   300	  extends AgentHooks<TContext, TOutput>
   301	  implements AgentConfiguration<TContext, TOutput>
   302	{
   303	  /**
   304	   * Create an Agent with handoffs and automatically infer the union type for TOutput from the handoff agents' output types.
   305	   */
   306	  static create<
   307	    TOutput extends AgentOutputType = TextOutput,
   308	    Handoffs extends readonly (Agent<any, any> | Handoff<any, any>)[] = [],
   309	  >(
   310	    config: AgentConfigWithHandoffs<TOutput, Handoffs>,
   311	  ): Agent<UnknownContext, TOutput | HandoffsOutputUnion<Handoffs>> {
   312	    return new Agent<UnknownContext, TOutput | HandoffsOutputUnion<Handoffs>>({
   313	      ...config,
   314	      handoffs: config.handoffs as any,
   315	      outputType: config.outputType,
   316	      handoffOutputTypeWarningEnabled: false,
   317	    });
   318	  }
   319	
   320	  static DEFAULT_MODEL_PLACEHOLDER = '';
   321	
   322	  name: string;
   323	  instructions:
   324	    | string
   325	    | ((
   326	        runContext: RunContext<TContext>,
   327	        agent: Agent<TContext, TOutput>,
   328	      ) => Promise<string> | string);
   329	  prompt?:
   330	    | Prompt
   331	    | ((
   332	        runContext: RunContext<TContext>,
   333	        agent: Agent<TContext, TOutput>,
   334	      ) => Promise<Prompt> | Prompt);
   335	  handoffDescription: string;
   336	  handoffs: (Agent<any, TOutput> | Handoff<any, TOutput>)[];
   337	  model: string | Model;
   338	  modelSettings: ModelSettings;
   339	  tools: Tool<TContext>[];
   340	  mcpServers: MCPServer[];
   341	  inputGuardrails: InputGuardrail[];
   342	  outputGuardrails: OutputGuardrail<AgentOutputType>[];
   343	  outputType: TOutput = 'text' as TOutput;
   344	  toolUseBehavior: ToolUseBehavior;
   345	  resetToolChoice: boolean;
   346	
   347	  constructor(config: AgentOptions<TContext, TOutput>) {
   348	    super();
   349	    if (typeof config.name !== 'string' || config.name.trim() === '') {
   350	      throw new UserError('Agent must have a name.');
   351	    }
   352	    this.name = config.name;
   353	    this.instructions = config.instructions ?? Agent.DEFAULT_MODEL_PLACEHOLDER;
   354	    this.prompt = config.prompt;
   355	    this.handoffDescription = config.handoffDescription ?? '';
   356	    this.handoffs = config.handoffs ?? [];
   357	    this.model = config.model ?? '';
   358	    this.modelSettings = config.modelSettings ?? getDefaultModelSettings();
   359	    this.tools = config.tools ?? [];
   360	    this.mcpServers = config.mcpServers ?? [];
   361	    this.inputGuardrails = config.inputGuardrails ?? [];
   362	    this.outputGuardrails = config.outputGuardrails ?? [];
   363	    if (config.outputType) {
   364	      this.outputType = config.outputType;
   365	    }
   366	    this.toolUseBehavior = config.toolUseBehavior ?? 'run_llm_again';
   367	    this.resetToolChoice = config.resetToolChoice ?? true;
   368	
   369	    if (
   370	      // The user sets a non-default model
   371	      config.model !== undefined &&
   372	      // The default model is gpt-5
   373	      isGpt5Default() &&
   374	      // However, the specified model is not a gpt-5 model
   375	      (typeof config.model !== 'string' ||
   376	        !gpt5ReasoningSettingsRequired(config.model)) &&
   377	      // The model settings are not customized for the specified model
   378	      config.modelSettings === undefined
   379	    ) {
   380	      // In this scenario, we should use a generic model settings
   381	      // because non-gpt-5 models are not compatible with the default gpt-5 model settings.
   382	      // This is a best-effort attempt to make the agent work with non-gpt-5 models.
   383	      this.modelSettings = {};
   384	    }
   385	
   386	    // --- Runtime warning for handoff output type compatibility ---
   387	    if (
   388	      config.handoffOutputTypeWarningEnabled === undefined ||
   389	      config.handoffOutputTypeWarningEnabled
   390	    ) {
   391	      if (this.handoffs && this.outputType) {
   392	        const outputTypes = new Set<string>([JSON.stringify(this.outputType)]);
   393	        for (const h of this.handoffs) {
   394	          if ('outputType' in h && h.outputType) {
   395	            outputTypes.add(JSON.stringify(h.outputType));
   396	          } else if ('agent' in h && h.agent.outputType) {
   397	            outputTypes.add(JSON.stringify(h.agent.outputType));
   398	          }
   399	        }
   400	        if (outputTypes.size > 1) {
   401	          logger.warn(
   402	            `[Agent] Warning: Handoff agents have different output types: ${Array.from(outputTypes).join(', ')}. You can make it type-safe by using Agent.create({ ... }) method instead.`,
   403	          );
   404	        }
   405	      }
   406	    }
   407	  }
   408	
   409	  /**
   410	   * Output schema name.
   411	   */
   412	  get outputSchemaName(): string {
   413	    if (this.outputType === 'text') {
   414	      return 'text';
   415	    } else if (isZodObject(this.outputType)) {
   416	      return 'ZodOutput';
   417	    } else if (typeof this.outputType === 'object') {
   418	      return this.outputType.name;
   419	    }
   420	
   421	    throw new Error(`Unknown output type: ${this.outputType}`);
   422	  }
   423	
   424	  /**
   425	   * Makes a copy of the agent, with the given arguments changed. For example, you could do:
   426	   *
   427	   * ```
   428	   * const newAgent = agent.clone({ instructions: 'New instructions' })
   429	   * ```
   430	   *
   431	   * @param config - A partial configuration to change.
   432	   * @returns A new agent with the given changes.
   433	   */
   434	  clone(
   435	    config: Partial<AgentConfiguration<TContext, TOutput>>,
   436	  ): Agent<TContext, TOutput> {
   437	    return new Agent({
   438	      ...this,
   439	      ...config,
   440	    });
   441	  }
   442	
   443	  /**
   444	   * Transform this agent into a tool, callable by other agents.
   445	   *
   446	   * This is different from handoffs in two ways:
   447	   * 1. In handoffs, the new agent receives the conversation history. In this tool, the new agent
   448	   *    receives generated input.
   449	   * 2. In handoffs, the new agent takes over the conversation. In this tool, the new agent is
   450	   *    called as a tool, and the conversation is continued by the original agent.
   451	   *
   452	   * @param options - Options for the tool.
   453	   * @returns A tool that runs the agent and returns the output text.
   454	   */
   455	  asTool(opti<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

    25	/**
    26	 * Data returned by the run() method of an agent.
    27	 */
    28	export interface RunResultData<
    29	  TAgent extends Agent<any, any>,
    30	  THandoffs extends (Agent<any, any> | Handoff<any>)[] = any[],
    31	> {
    32	  /**
    33	   * The original input items i.e. the items before run() was called. This may be mutated version
    34	   * of the input, if there are handoff input filters that mutate the input.
    35	   */
    36	  input: string | AgentInputItem[];
    37	
    38	  /**
    39	   * The new items generated during the agent run. These include things like new messages, tool
    40	   * calls and their outputs, etc.
    41	   */
    42	  newItems: RunItem[];
    43	
    44	  /**
    45	   * The raw LLM responses generated by the model during the agent run.
    46	   */
    47	  rawResponses: ModelResponse[];
    48	
    49	  /**
    50	   * The last response ID generated by the model during the agent run.
    51	   */
    52	  lastResponseId: string | undefined;
    53	
    54	  /**
    55	   * The last agent that was run
    56	   */
    57	  lastAgent: TAgent | undefined;
    58	
    59	  /**
    60	   * Guardrail results for the input messages.
    61	   */
    62	  inputGuardrailResults: InputGuardrailResult[];
    63	
    64	  /**
    65	   * Guardrail results for the final output of the agent.
    66	   */
    67	  outputGuardrailResults: OutputGuardrailResult[];
    68	
    69	  /**
    70	   * The output of the last agent, or any handoff agent.
    71	   */
    72	  finalOutput?:
    73	    | ResolvedAgentOutput<TAgent['outputType']>
    74	    | HandoffsOutput<THandoffs>;
    75	
    76	  /**
    77	   * The interruptions that occurred during the agent run.
    78	   */
    79	  interruptions?: RunToolApprovalItem[];
    80	
    81	  /**
    82	   * The state of the run.
    83	   */
    84	  state: RunState<any, TAgent>;
    85	}
    86	
    87	class RunResultBase<TContext, TAgent extends Agent<TContext, any>>
    88	  implements RunResultData<TAgent>
    89	{
    90	  readonly state: RunState<TContext, TAgent>;
    91	
    92	  constructor(state: RunState<TContext, TAgent>) {
    93	    this.state = state;
    94	  }
    95	
    96	  /**
    97	   * The history of the agent run. This includes the input items and the new items generated during
    98	   * the agent run.
    99	   *
   100	   * This can be used as inputs for the next agent run.
   101	   */
   102	  get history(): AgentInputItem[] {
   103	    return getTurnInput(this.input, this.newItems);
   104	  }
   105	
   106	  /**
   107	   * The new items generated during the agent run. These include things like new messages, tool
   108	   * calls and their outputs, etc.
   109	   *
   110	   * It does not include information about the agents and instead represents the model data.
   111	   *
   112	   * For the output including the agents, use the `newItems` property.
   113	   */
   114	  get output(): AgentOutputItem[] {
   115	    return getTurnInput([], this.newItems);
   116	  }
   117	
   118	  /**
   119	   * A copy of the original input items.
   120	   */
   121	  get input(): string | AgentInputItem[] {
   122	    return this.state._originalInput;
   123	  }
   124	
   125	  /**
   126	   * The run items generated during the agent run. This associates the model data with the agents.
   127	   *
   128	   * For the model data that can be used as inputs for the next agent run, use the `output` property.
   129	   */
   130	  get newItems(): RunItem[] {
   131	    return this.state._generatedItems;
   132	  }
   133	
   134	  /**
   135	   * The raw LLM responses generated by the model during the agent run.
   136	   */
   137	  get rawResponses(): ModelResponse[] {
   138	    return this.state._modelResponses;
   139	  }
   140	
   141	  /**
   142	   * The last response ID generated by the model during the agent run.
   143	   */
   144	  get lastResponseId(): string | undefined {
   145	    const responses = this.rawResponses;
   146	    return responses && responses.length > 0
   147	      ? responses[responses.length - 1].responseId
   148	      : undefined;
   149	  }
   150	
   151	  /**
   152	   * The last agent that was run
   153	   */
   154	  get lastAgent(): TAgent | undefined {
   155	    return this.state._currentAgent;
   156	  }
   157	
   158	  /**
   159	   * Guardrail results for the input messages.
   160	   */
   161	  get inputGuardrailResults(): InputGuardrailResult[] {
   162	    return this.state._inputGuardrailResults;
   163	  }
   164	
   165	  /**
   166	   * Guardrail results for the final output of the agent.
   167	   */
   168	  get outputGuardrailResults(): OutputGuardrailResult[] {
   169	    return this.state._outputGuardrailResults;
   170	  }
   171	
   172	  /**
   173	   * Any interruptions that occurred during the agent run for example for tool approvals.
   174	   */
   175	  get interruptions(): RunToolApprovalItem[] {
   176	    if (this.state._currentStep?.type === 'next_step_interruption') {
   177	      return this.state._currentStep.data.interruptions;
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    return [];
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  /**
   184	   * The final output of the agent. If the output type was set to anything other than `text`,
   185	   * this will be parsed either as JSON or using the Zod schema you provided.
   186	   */
   187	  get finalOutput(): ResolvedAgentOutput<TAgent['outputType']> | undefined {
   188	    if (this.state._currentStep?.type === 'next_step_final_output') {
   189	      return this.state._currentAgent.processFinalOutput(
   190	        this.state._currentStep.output,
   191	      ) as ResolvedAgentOutput<TAgent['outputType']>;
   192	    }
   193	
   194	    logger.warn('Accessed finalOutput before agent run is completed.');
   195	    return undefined;
   196	  }
   197	}
   198	
   199	/**
   200	 * The result of an agent run.
   201	 */
   202	export class RunResult<
   203	  TContext,
   204	  TAgent extends Agent<TContext, AgentOutputType>,
   205	> extends RunResultBase<TContext, TAgent> {
   206	  constructor(state: RunState<TContext, TAgent>) {
   207	    super(state);
   208	  }
   209	}
   210	
   211	/**
   212	 * The result of an agent run in streaming mode.
   213	 */
   214	export class StreamedRunResult<
   215	    TContext,
   216	    TAgent extends Agent<TContext, AgentOutputType>,
   217	  >
   218	  extends RunResultBase<TContext, TAgent>
   219	  implements AsyncIterable<RunStreamEvent>
   220	{
   221	  /**
   222	   * The current agent that is running
   223	   */
   224	  public get currentAgent(): TAgent | undefined {
   225	    return this.lastAgent;
   226	  }
   227	
   228	  /**
   229	   * The current turn number
   230	   */
   231	  public currentTurn: number = 0;
   232	
   233	  /**
   234	   * The maximum number of turns that can be run
   235	   */
   236	  public maxTurns: number | undefined;
   237	
   238	  #error: unknown = null;
   239	  #signal?: AbortSignal;
   240	  #readableController: ReadableStreamController<RunStreamEvent> | undefined;
   241	  #readableStream: _ReadableStream<RunStreamEvent>;
   242	  #completedPromise: Promise<void>;
   243	  #completedPromiseResolve: (() => void) | undefined;
   244	  #completedPromiseReject: ((err: unknown) => void) | undefined;
   245	  #cancelled: boolean = false;
   246	
   247	  constructor(
   248	    result: {
   249	      state: RunState<TContext, TAgent>;
   250	      signal?: AbortSignal;
   251	    } = {} as any,
   252	  ) {
   253	    super(result.state);
   254	
   255	    this.#signal = result.signal;
   256	
   257	    if (this.#signal) {
   258	      this.#signal.addEventListener('abort', async () => {
   259	        await this.#readableStream.cancel();
   260	      });
   261	    }
   262	
   263	    this.#readableStream = new _ReadableStream<RunStreamEvent>({
   264	      start: (controller) => {
   265	        this.#readableController = controller;
   266	      },
   267	      cancel: () => {
   268	        this.#cancelled = true;
   269	      },
   270	    });
   271	
   272	    this.#completedPromise = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   273	      this.#completedPromiseResolve = resolve;
   274	      this.#completedPromiseReject = reject;
   275	    });
   276	  }
   277	
   278	  /**
   279	   * @internal
   280	   * Adds an item to the stream of output items
   281	   */
   282	  _addItem(item: RunStreamEvent) {
   283	    if (!this.cancelled) {
   284	      this.#readableController?.enqueue(item);
   285	    }
   286	  }
   287	
   288	  /**
   289	   * @internal
   290	   * Indicates that the stream has been completed
   291	   */
   292	  _done() {
   293	    if (!this.cancelled && this.#readableController) {
   294	      this.#readableController.close();
   295	      this.#readableController = undefined;
   296	      this.#completedPromiseResolve?.();
   297	    }
   298	  }
   299	
   300	  /**
   301	   * @internal
   302	   * Handles an error in the stream loop.
   303	   */
   304	  _raiseError(err: unknown) {
   305	    if (!this.cancelled && this.#readableController) {
   306	      this.#readableController.error(err);
   307	      this.#readableController = undefined;
   308	    }
   309	    this.#error = err;
   310	    this.#completedPromiseReject?.(err);
   311	    this.#completedPromise.catch((e) => {
   312	      logger.debug(`Resulted in an error: ${e}`);
   313	    });
   314	  }
   315	
   316	  /**
   317	   * Returns true if the stream has been cancelled.
   318	   */
   319	  get cancelled(): boolean {
   320	    return this.#cancelled;
   321	  }
   322	
   323	  /**
   324	   * Returns the underlying readable stream.
   325	   * @returns A readable stream of the agent run.
   326	   */
   327	  toStream(): ReadableStream<RunStreamEvent> {
   328	    return this.#readableStream as ReadableStream<RunStreamEvent>;
   329	  }
   330	
   331	  /**
   332	   * Await this promise to ensure that the stream has been completed if you are not consuming the
   333	   * stream directly.
   334	   */
   335	  get completed() {
   336	    return this.#completedPromise;
   337	  }
   338	
   339	  /**
   340	   * Error thrown during the run, if any.
   341	   */
   342	  get error() {
   343	    return this.#error;
   344	  }
   345	
   346	  /**
   347	   * Returns a readable stream of the final text output of the agent run.
   348	   *
   349	   * @param options - Options for the stream.
   350	   * @param options.compatibleWithNodeStreams - Whether to use Node.js streams or web standard streams.
   351	   * @returns A readable stream of the final output of the agent run.
   352	   */
   353	  toTextStream(): ReadableStream<string>;
   354	  toTextStream(options?: { compatibleWithNodeStreams: true }): Readable;
   355	  toTextStream(options?: {
   356	    compatibleWithNodeStreams?: false;
   357	  }): ReadableStream<string>;
   358	  toTextStream(
   359	    options: { compatibleWithNodeStreams?: boolean } = {},
   360	  ): Readable | ReadableStream<string> {
   361	    const stream = this.#readableStream.pipeThrough(
   362	      new TransformStream<RunStreamEvent, string>({
   363	        transform(event, controller) {
   364	          if (
   365	            event.type === 'raw_model_stream_event' &&
   366	            event.data.type === 'output_text_delta'
   367	          ) {
   368	            const item = StreamEventTextStream.parse(event.data);
   369	            controller.enqueue(item.delta);
   370	          }
   371	        },
   372	      }),
   373	    );
   374	
   375	    if (options.compatibleWithNodeStreams) {
   376	      return Readable.fromWeb(stream);
   377	    }
   378	
   379	    return stream as ReadableStream<string>;
   380	  }
   381	
   382	  [Symbol.asyncIterator](): AsyncIterator<RunStreamEvent> {
   383	    return this.#readableStream[Symbol.asyncIterator]();
   384	  }
   385	}

async function repro() {
  const mockModel = new MockModel();
  const myAgent = new Agent({
    name: '"'"'My Agent'"'"',
    instructions: '"'"'Some instructions'"'"',
    model: mockModel,
    outputType: '"'"'text'"'"',
  });
  const runner = new Runner();
  
  let agentEndCalled = false;
  myAgent.on('"'"'agent_end'"'"', (context, output) => {
    console.log('"'"'agent_end called'"'"');
    agentEndCalled = true;
  });

  console.log('"'"'Running non-streaming agent...'"'"');
  await runner.run(myAgent, '"'"'hi'"'"', { stream: false });
  console.log('"'"'Non-streaming agent_end called:'"'"', agentEndCalled);

  agentEndCalled = false;
  console.log('"'"'\nRunning streaming agent...'"'"');

    stream: true
  });

    if (event.type === '"'"'raw_model_stream_event'"'"' && event.data.type === '"'"'response_done'"'"') {

    }
  }
  console.log('"'"'Streaming agent_end called:'"'"', agentEndCalled);
}'

import { Agent } from './packages/agents-core/src/agent';
import { Runner } from './packages/agents-core/src/run';
import { Model, ModelResponse } from './packages/agents-core/src/model';
import * as protocol from './packages/agents-core/src/types/protocol';
import { setDefaultModelProvider } from './packages/agents-core/src/providers';
setDefaultModelProvider({ getModel: () => ({} as any) });

class MockModel implements Model {
  async getResponse(): Promise<ModelResponse> {
    return {
      output: [{ type: 'message', role: 'assistant', content: 'Hello' }],
      usage: { promptTokens: 0, completionTokens: 0, totalTokens: 0 } as any,
    };
  }
  async *getStreamedResponse(): AsyncGenerator<protocol.StreamEvent> {
    yield {
        type: 'response_done',
        response: {
            id: 'resp-1',
            usage: { prompt_tokens: 10, completion_tokens: 20, total_tokens: 30 },
            output: [{ type: 'message', role: 'assistant', content: 'Hello' }],
        }
    } as any;
  }
}

async function repro() {
  const mockModel = new MockModel();
  const myAgent = new Agent({
    name: 'My Agent',
    instructions: 'Some instructions',
    model: mockModel,
    outputType: 'text',
    toolUseBehavior: () => ({ isFinalOutput: true, finalOutput: 'Hello', isInterrupted: undefined })
  });
  const runner = new Runner();
  
  let agentEndCalled = false;
  myAgent.on('agent_end', (context, output) => {
    console.log('agent_end called');
    agentEndCalled = true;
  });

  console.log('Running non-streaming agent...');
  await runner.run(myAgent, 'hi', { stream: false });
  console.log('Non-streaming agent_end called:', agentEndCalled);

  agentEndCalled = false;
  console.log('\nRunning streaming agent...');
  const streamResult = await runner.run(myAgent, 'hi', {
    stream: true
  });
  
  for await (const event of streamResult) {
    if (event.type === 'raw_model_stream_event' && event.data.type === 'response_done') {
        const item = event.data as any;
        item.response.output = [{ type: 'message', role: 'assistant', content: 'Hello' }];
    }
  }
  console.log('Streaming agent_end called:', agentEndCalled);
}

repro().catch(console.error);
